  <script>
   (function () {
  'use strict';

  var requestAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame || window.mozRequestAnimationFrame || window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame || window.msRequestAnimationFrame;
  var deferredCssElement = document.getElementById('deferred-css');
  var cssLoadListeners = [];
  var isCssLoaded;

  if (deferredCssElement === null) {
    isCssLoaded = true;
  } else {
    isCssLoaded = false;

    document.body.addEventListener('load', handleLoadEvent, true);

    if (requestAnimationFrame) {
      requestAnimationFrame(function () {
        window.setTimeout(loadDeferredCss, 0);
      });
    } else {
      window.addEventListener('load', loadDeferredCss);
    }
  }

  window.addCssLoadEventListener = function (listener) {
    if (isCssLoaded) {
      listener();
    } else {
      cssLoadListeners.push(listener);
    }
  };

  function loadDeferredCss() {
    var divElement = document.createElement('div');

    if (deferredCssElement) {
      divElement.innerHTML = deferredCssElement.textContent;
      document.body.appendChild(divElement);
      deferredCssElement.parentElement.removeChild(deferredCssElement);
    }
  }

  function handleLoadEvent(event) {
    var preLoaderCssElement;

    if (event && event.target && event.target.className === 'css') {
      isCssLoaded = true;

      preLoaderCssElement = document.getElementById('preloader-css');
      if (preLoaderCssElement !== null) {
        preLoaderCssElement.parentNode.removeChild(preLoaderCssElement);
      }

      cssLoadListeners.forEach(function (listener) {
        listener();
      });
    }
  }
}());

  function createRegexVendorMap(vendorMap) {
    var mapWithRegexes = {};
    for (var libraryName in vendorMap) {
      if (!vendorMap.hasOwnProperty(libraryName)) {
        continue;
      }
      mapWithRegexes[['vendor', libraryName].join('/')] = {
        'versioned': vendorMap[libraryName],
        'regexp': new RegExp('^vendor/' + libraryName + '/')
      };
    }
    return mapWithRegexes;
  }

  function getVersioned(input, mapWithRegexes) {

      if (!input.match(regexp)) {
        continue;
      }
      versioned = mapWithRegexes[source].versioned + '/';
      return input.replace(regexp, versioned);
    }
    return input;
  }

  function mapPaths(paths) {
    var mappedPaths = {};
    for (var alias in paths) {
      if (!paths.hasOwnProperty(alias)) {
        continue;
      }
      mappedPaths[alias] = getVersioned(paths[alias], mapWithRegexes);
    }
    for (var libraryName in mapWithRegexes) {
      if (!mapWithRegexes.hasOwnProperty(libraryName)) {
        continue;
      }
      mappedPaths[libraryName] = mapWithRegexes[libraryName].versioned;
    }
    return mappedPaths;
  }

  nd.auto = nd.auto || {};

  /**
   * @deprecated
   */
  nd.auto.define = define;

  nd.auto.require = requirejs.config({
    context: 'auto',
    waitSeconds: 60,
    baseUrl: jsBaseUrl,
    paths: paths,
    shim: shim,

      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.core.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.autoheight.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.caption.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.command.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.pager.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.prevnext.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/core/jquery.cycle2.tmpl.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/plugin/jquery.cycle2.swipe.min',
      'vendor/jquery-cycle2-gforces/build/plugin/jquery.cycle2.carousel.min',
      'vendor/bootstrap/dist/js/bootstrap.min',
      'vendor/bootstrap-select/dist/js/bootstrap-select.min'
    ],
    callback: function (requestFrame, scriptsRunner) {
      'use strict';

      requestFrame('native');
      scriptsRunner();
    }
  });

  nd.auto.require(['main/main'], function (main) {
    'use strict';
    main();
  });

  if (nd.auto.requireQueue &amp;&amp; nd.auto.requireQueue.length) {
    nd.auto.requireQueue.forEach(function (queuedRequire) {
      nd.auto.require(queuedRequire.deps, queuedRequire.callback);
    });
  }

         <section class="inner">
          <div class="row-fluid">
           <div class="text span12">
            <div class="textInner">
             <h1>
              Marshall Motor Group
              <br/>
             </h1>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="row-fluid">
           <div class="text span12">
            <div class="textInner">
             <p>
              <strong>
               Established for over 100 years, the Marshall Motor Group helps customers across Great Britain to find their next new or used car, van, bike or even a truck!
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              With locations spanning from Plymouth in the south to Scarborough in the north, the chances are that youre within a short drive of your nearest dealership. Every single location is committed to upholding our Six Pillars of customer service, ensuring every Marshall Motor Group customer experiences the same high quality of care at every point.
             </p>
             <p>
              Were proud to be one of the UKs largest dealer networks, working with many of the most popular car brands. Whether youre looking for an elegant executive vehicle, luxurious sports car or compact urban runaround, well offer a car that more than meets your needs. As well as brand new cars, motorcycles and
              <span class="text" style="background-color: initial;">
               vans
              </span>
              , we have a comprehensive selection of
              <a class="cms-link" data-label-text="used cars" data-page-id="" data-section-id="" data-selected-type="" data-target="" data-type="link" data-url="/used-cars/" href="/used-cars/" rel="follow" target="">
               <span class="text">
                used cars
               </span>
              </a>
              and commercial vehicles available at locations across the country. Our current inventory of used models is available to browse online today. You can search for
              <a class="cms-link" data-label-text="used cars in your area" data-page-id="" data-section-id="" data-selected-type="" data-target="" data-type="link" data-url="/used-cars/location-search/" href="/used-cars/location-search/" rel="follow" target="">
               <span class="text">
                used cars in your area
               </span>
              </a>
              or by the brand of your choice.
             </p>
             <p>
              We can also help you ensure your car or van leads a long and reliable life, thanks to manufacturer-backed servicing and maintenance at competitive prices. We can also help you get your vehicle prepared for its MOT or repaired following an accident.
             </p>
             <p>
              Flexible finance is offered on every vehicle we sell, and we have experts at every dealership who can talk you through the relative merits of the different agreement types. Our fleet specialists can also help if youre looking for an affordable bank of vehicles for your employees to use.
             </p>
             <p>
              Were delighted to be able to help customers access the Motability Scheme with many of the brands we represent. We can help you check if youre eligible and then guide you through the ordering process, from identifying the right model to getting adaptations fitted.
             </p>
             <p>
              You find
              <a class="cms-link" data-label-text="contact details" data-page-id="" data-section-id="" data-selected-type="" data-target="" data-type="link" data-url="/contact-us/" href="/contact-us/" rel="follow" target="">
               <span class="text">
                contact details
               </span>
              </a>
              for your nearest Marshall dealer by navigating the site today. We look forward to hearing from you.
              <br/>
             </p>

        nd.auto.require(["jquery"], function () {
        $("img.css-bg-image").show();
        updateBackgroundImages();
        window.onresize = function(event) { updateBackgroundImages(); };

        function updateBackgroundImages() {
            var windowWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
            var device = "desktop";
            if (windowWidth <= 767) device = "mobile";

            var backgroundImages = document.querySelectorAll(".css-bg-image");
            for (var i = 0; i < backgroundImages.length; i++) {
                backgroundImages[i].src = backgroundImages[i].getAttribute("data-" + device + "-src");
            }
        }
        });
